from ddgs import DDGS
import json
import os
from datetime import datetime

# Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist
if not os.path.exists('workspace'):
    os.makedirs('workspace')
    print("ðŸ“ Created workspace directory")
else:
    print("ðŸ“ Workspace directory exists")

print("ðŸŽ¼ ANDRÃ‰ MATHIEU BIRTHPLACE RESEARCH - FRENCH DEPARTMENT IDENTIFICATION")

print("Research Objective: Find the specific French department where AndrÃ© Mathieu was born")
print("Target: Canadian composer (1929-1968) whose works were used for 1976 Montreal Olympics")
print("Focus: Biographical details and French administrative division identification")

# Define targeted search queries for AndrÃ© Mathieu's birthplace in France
search_queries = [
    'AndrÃ© Mathieu composer birthplace France department',
    'AndrÃ© Mathieu born France which department',
    'AndrÃ© Mathieu biography birth location French department',
    'AndrÃ© Mathieu Canadian composer born France where',
    '"AndrÃ© Mathieu" composer France birth department',
    'AndrÃ© Mathieu 1929 birth France department region',
    'AndrÃ© Mathieu Montreal Olympics composer birthplace France',

]

# Initialize search engine with multiple backends for reliability
searcher = DDGS(timeout=15)
backends = ["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yandex", "brave"]

# Store all search results for comprehensive analysis
all_results = []
successful_searches = 0
failed_searches = 0

# Execute searches with detailed progress tracking

    print(f"\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}")
    print("-" * 70)
    
    try:
        # Perform search with multiple backend fallback
        results = searcher.text(
            query, 
            max_results=10, 
            page=1, 
            backend=backends, 
            safesearch="off", 
            region="en-us"
        )
        
        if results and len(results) > 0:
            print(f"âœ… Found {len(results)} results for search {i}")
            successful_searches += 1
            
            # Process and analyze each result immediately
            for j, result in enumerate(results, 1):
                try:
                    title = result.get('title', 'No title')
                    href = result.get('href', 'No link')
                    body = result.get('body', 'No snippet')
                    
                    print(f"\nResult {j}:")
                    print(f"Title: {title}")
                    print(f"Link: {href}")
                    print(f"Snippet: {body[:250]}..." if len(body) > 250 else f"Snippet: {body}")

                    title_lower = title.lower() if title else ''
                    body_lower = body.lower() if body else ''

                    mathieu_indicators = ['andrÃ© mathieu', 'andre mathieu', 'mathieu']
                    birth_indicators = ['born', 'birth', 'birthplace', 'born in', 'birth in', 'nÃ©', 'naissance']
                    france_indicators = ['france', 'french', 'franÃ§ais', 'franÃ§aise']
                    department_indicators = ['department', 'dÃ©partement', 'region', 'rÃ©gion', 'province']
                    composer_indicators = ['composer', 'compositeur', 'pianist', 'pianiste', 'musician', 'musicien']
                    date_indicators = ['1929', '1968', 'montreal', 'olympics', 'olympiques']
                    
                    # Count matches for comprehensive relevance scoring
                    mathieu_matches = [ind for ind in mathieu_indicators if ind in combined_content]
                    birth_matches = [ind for ind in birth_indicators if ind in combined_content]
                    france_matches = [ind for ind in france_indicators if ind in combined_content]
                    dept_matches = [ind for ind in department_indicators if ind in combined_content]
                    composer_matches = [ind for ind in composer_indicators if ind in combined_content]
                    date_matches = [ind for ind in date_indicators if ind in combined_content]
                    
                    total_relevance = len(mathieu_matches) + len(birth_matches) + len(france_matches) + len(dept_matches) + len(composer_matches) + len(date_matches)
                    
                    # Display detailed relevance analysis

                        print(f"ðŸ‘¤ MATHIEU MATCH: {mathieu_matches}")
                    if birth_matches:
                        print(f"ðŸŽ‚ BIRTH MATCH: {birth_matches}")
                    if france_matches:
                        print(f"ðŸ‡«ðŸ‡· FRANCE MATCH: {france_matches}")
                    if dept_matches:
                        print(f"ðŸ“ DEPARTMENT MATCH: {dept_matches}")
                    if composer_matches:
                        print(f"ðŸŽ¼ COMPOSER MATCH: {composer_matches}")
                    if date_matches:
                        print(f"ðŸ“… DATE MATCH: {date_matches}")

                        print(f"â­ HIGH RELEVANCE SCORE: {total_relevance}")
                    elif total_relevance >= 2:
                        print(f"âœ“ Potentially relevant: {total_relevance}")
                    
                    # Look for specific French department names in content
                    french_departments = [
                        'paris', 'seine', 'hauts-de-seine', 'seine-saint-denis', 'val-de-marne',
                        'yvelines', 'essonne', 'val-d\'oise', 'loire', 'rhÃ´ne', 'isÃ¨re',
                        'bouches-du-rhÃ´ne', 'var', 'alpes-maritimes', 'nord', 'pas-de-calais',
                        'gironde', 'haute-garonne', 'hÃ©rault', 'loire-atlantique', 'ille-et-vilaine'
                    ]

                    if canadian_matches:
                        print(f"ðŸ CANADIAN CONNECTION: {canadian_matches}")

                    print(f"âŒ Error processing result {j}: {str(result_error)}")

import os
import json
from datetime import datetime

# First, let's inspect the workspace directory to understand what files exist
workspace_dir = 'workspace'
if os.path.exists(workspace_dir):
    print(f"ðŸ“ Workspace directory contents:")
    files = os.listdir(workspace_dir)
    for file in files:
        file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, file)
        file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path)
        print(f"  - {file} ({file_size} bytes)")
    print()
else:
    print("ðŸ“ Workspace directory does not exist")
    os.makedirs(workspace_dir)
    print("ðŸ“ Created workspace directory")

# Look for AndrÃ© Mathieu related files
mathieu_files = [f for f in os.listdir(workspace_dir) if 'andre_mathieu' in f.lower() or 'mathieu' in f.lower()]
print(f"ðŸ“„ AndrÃ© Mathieu related files found: {len(mathieu_files)}")
for file in mathieu_files:
    print(f"  - {file}")

# If there are existing files, let's inspect their structure first

    # Take the most recent or relevant file
    latest_file = mathieu_files[0]  # We'll inspect the first one
    file_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, latest_file)

        if latest_file.endswith('.json'):
            with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                data = json.load(f)
            
            print(f"ðŸ“Š JSON file structure:")
            if isinstance(data, dict):
                print(f"Top-level keys:")
                for key in data.keys():
                    value = data[key]
                    print(f"  - {key}: {type(value)} - {str(value)[:100]}{'...' if len(str(value)) > 100 else ''}")
                
                # If there's a results key, inspect its structure
                if 'results' in data and data['results']:
                    print(f"\nðŸ“‹ Results structure (first result):")

                        print(f"  - {key}: {type(value)} = {str(value)[:150]}{'...' if len(str(value)) > 150 else ''}")

# Now let's conduct a proper verification search about AndrÃ© Mathieu's actual birthplace
from ddgs import DDGS

print(f"\nðŸ” VERIFICATION SEARCH: AndrÃ© Mathieu's Actual Birthplace")
print("=" * 60)

# Define verification queries to confirm birthplace
verification_queries = [
    'AndrÃ© Mathieu Canadian composer born Montreal biography',
    'AndrÃ© Mathieu birthplace Montreal Canada composer pianist',
    'AndrÃ© Mathieu 1929 birth Montreal Quebec biographical facts',
    '"AndrÃ© Mathieu" "born in Montreal" Canadian composer biography'
]

searcher = DDGS(timeout=15)
backends = ["google", "duckduckgo", "bing"]

verification_results = []
successful_verifications = 0

for i, query in enumerate(verification_queries, 1):
    print(f"\nVerification {i}/{len(verification_queries)}: {query}")
    print("-" * 65)
    
    try:
        results = searcher.text(
            query, 
            max_results=5, 
            page=1, 
            backend=backends, 
            safesearch="off", 
            region="en-us"
        )
        
        if results and len(results) > 0:
            print(f"âœ… Found {len(results)} verification results")
            successful_verifications += 1
            
            for j, result in enumerate(results, 1):
                title = result.get('title', 'No title')
                href = result.get('href', 'No link')
                body = result.get('body', 'No snippet')
                
                print(f"\nResult {j}:")
                print(f"Title: {title}")
                print(f"Link: {href}")
                print(f"Snippet: {body[:200]}..." if len(body) > 200 else f"Snippet: {body}")
                
                # Check for key birthplace indicators
                content_lower = f"{title.lower()} {body.lower()}"
                montreal_mentions = 'montreal' in content_lower
                canada_mentions = 'canada' in content_lower or 'canadian' in content_lower
                quebec_mentions = 'quebec' in content_lower
                birth_mentions = 'born' in content_lower or 'birth' in content_lower
                date_mentions = '1929' in content_lower
                
                if montreal_mentions:
                    print(f"ðŸ™ï¸ MONTREAL CONFIRMED")
                if canada_mentions:
                    print(f"ðŸ‡¨ðŸ‡¦ CANADA CONFIRMED")
                if quebec_mentions:
                    print(f"ðŸ QUEBEC CONFIRMED")
                if birth_mentions:
                    print(f"ðŸŽ‚ BIRTH REFERENCE CONFIRMED")
                if date_mentions:
                    print(f"ðŸ“… 1929 DATE CONFIRMED")
                
                verification_results.append({
                    'query': query,
                    'title': title,
                    'href': href,
                    'body': body,
                    'montreal_confirmed': montreal_mentions,
                    'canada_confirmed': canada_mentions,
                    'quebec_confirmed': quebec_mentions,
                    'birth_confirmed': birth_mentions,
                    'date_confirmed': date_mentions
                })
                
                print("-" * 40)
        else:
            print(f"âŒ No results for verification {i}")
    
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"âŒ Error during verification {i}: {str(e)}")
        continue

# Compile final verified information
print(f"\n\nðŸ“Š VERIFICATION SUMMARY:")
print("=" * 30)
print(f"Verification queries executed: {len(verification_queries)}")
print(f"Successful verifications: {successful_verifications}")
print(f"Total verification results: {len(verification_results)}")

# Count confirmations

```
### Development Step 17: Search French-Origin Pioneer Pictures Composers of 1976 Montreal Olympics Theme Music.

**Description**: Re-examine the original TASK requirements and search for alternative composers who both worked for Pioneer Pictures and composed theme music for the 1976 Montreal Olympics. The previous research focused on AndrÃ© Mathieu who was born in Canada, not France, which doesn't match the TASK criteria. Search for other composers associated with the 1976 Montreal Olympics who might have French origins and Pioneer Pictures connections, including any secondary composers, arrangers, or musicians involved in the Olympic ceremonies who had film industry backgrounds.

**Use Cases**:
- Film archival teams automating the cross-referencing of composer credits between Pioneer Pictures archives and the 1976 Montreal Olympic ceremony records
- Academic musicology researchers compiling a dataset of French-born composers who scored Olympic event music for a doctoral thesis
- Sports event organizers scouting composers with prior Olympic ceremony experience and film studio backgrounds for upcoming opening ceremonies
- Music licensing departments automating the identification of copyright holders of Olympic theme tracks produced by Pioneer Picturesâ€“affiliated French artists
- Cultural heritage institutions enriching digital archives by linking Pioneer Pictures film scores to Montreal 1976 Olympic ceremonies through web-based search analysis
- Documentary producers sourcing interview candidates by finding secondary or orchestration composers involved in the 1976 Olympics music team with French origins
- Genealogy researchers tracing the career trajectories of French-emigrant composers who worked for Pioneer Pictures and contributed to major sporting event soundtracks
- Music festival programmers curating themed concert series featuring Olympic compositions by French film composers, using automated search to uncover obscure artist names

```
import os
import json
import requests
from urllib.parse import quote
import re

print("=== ALTERNATIVE COMPOSER SEARCH: 1976 MONTREAL OLYMPICS ===\n")
print("Objective: Find French-born composers with Pioneer Pictures connections")
print("Focus: Alternative to AndrÃ© Mathieu who was Canadian, not French\n")

# Search queries targeting French composers and 1976 Montreal Olympics
search_queries = [
    "1976 Montreal Olympics theme music composer French born Pioneer Pictures",
    "Montreal 1976 Olympics ceremony music French composer film industry",
    "Pioneer Pictures composer 1976 Olympics Montreal French musician",
    "1976 Montreal Olympics opening ceremony music French composer arranger",
    "French composer 1976 Montreal Olympics theme Pioneer Pictures background",
    "Montreal Olympics 1976 secondary composers French film music Pioneer",
    "1976 Olympics Montreal music team French composers film industry connections",
    "Pioneer Pictures French composer Olympic theme music 1976 Montreal"
]

# Get SerpAPI key from environment variables
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key is None:
    print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.")
else:
    print(f"Starting comprehensive search with {len(search_queries)} different query approaches\n")
    
    all_search_results = []
    
    for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1):
        print(f"=== SEARCH {i}/{len(search_queries)} ===")
        print(f"Query: {query}")
        
        # Prepare API request parameters
        params = {
            "q": query,
            "api_key": api_key,
            "engine": "google",
            "google_domain": "google.com",
            "safe": "off",
            "num": 15,  # Get more results for comprehensive search
            "type": "search",
        }
        
        try:
            # Make API request to SerpAPI
            response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30)
            
            if response.status_code == 200:
                results = response.json()
                print(f"Search successful - found {len(results.get('organic_results', []))} organic results")
                
                # Store results with query context
                search_result = {
                    'query_number': i,
                    'query_text': query,
                    'results_data': results,
                    'organic_count': len(results.get('organic_results', []))
                }
                all_search_results.append(search_result)
                
                # Analyze results for relevant keywords immediately
                if results.get("organic_results"):
                    print("\nAnalyzing results for French composers and Pioneer Pictures connections:\n")
                    
                    for j, result in enumerate(results['organic_results'][:10], 1):  # Check first 10 results
                        title = result.get('title', 'No title')
                        link = result.get('link', 'No link')
                        snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')
                        
                        combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower()
                        
                        print(f"Result {j}:")
                        print(f"Title: {title}")
                        print(f"URL: {link}")
                        print(f"Snippet: {snippet[:200]}{'...' if len(snippet) > 200 else ''}")
                        
                        # Look for French origin indicators
                        french_keywords = ['french', 'france', 'born in france', 'french composer', 'paris', 'lyon', 'marseille']
                        found_french_keywords = [kw for kw in french_keywords if kw in combined_text]
                        
                        # Look for Pioneer Pictures connections
                        pioneer_keywords = ['pioneer pictures', 'pioneer', 'film studio', 'movie studio', 'film industry']
                        found_pioneer_keywords = [kw for kw in pioneer_keywords if kw in combined_text]
                        
                        # Look for 1976 Montreal Olympics references
                        olympics_keywords = ['1976', 'montreal', 'olympics', 'olympic', 'ceremony', 'opening ceremony']
                        found_olympics_keywords = [kw for kw in olympics_keywords if kw in combined_text]
                        
                        # Look for composer/music keywords
                        music_keywords = ['composer', 'music', 'theme', 'soundtrack', 'score', 'musician', 'arranger']
                        found_music_keywords = [kw for kw in music_keywords if kw in combined_text]
                        
                        # Highlight significant matches
                        if found_french_keywords:
                            print(f"*** FRENCH ORIGIN KEYWORDS: {', '.join(found_french_keywords)} ***")
                        
                        if found_pioneer_keywords:
                            print(f"*** PIONEER PICTURES KEYWORDS: {', '.join(found_pioneer_keywords)} ***")
                        
                        if found_olympics_keywords:
                            print(f"*** 1976 MONTREAL OLYMPICS KEYWORDS: {', '.join(found_olympics_keywords)} ***")
                        
                        if found_music_keywords:
                            print(f"*** MUSIC/COMPOSER KEYWORDS: {', '.join(found_music_keywords)} ***")
                        
                        # Calculate relevance score
                        relevance_score = len(found_french_keywords) + len(found_pioneer_keywords) + len(found_olympics_keywords) + len(found_music_keywords)
                        if relevance_score >= 3:
                            print(f"*** HIGH RELEVANCE RESULT (Score: {relevance_score}/4) ***")
                        
                        # Look for specific composer names
                        name_patterns = [
                            r'composer\s+([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)',
                            r'([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)\s+composer',
                            r'music by\s+([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)',
                            r'([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+).*french',
                            r'french.*([A-Z][a-z]+\s+[A-Z][a-z]+)'
                        ]
                        
                        for pattern in name_patterns:
                            matches = re.findall(pattern, snippet, re.IGNORECASE)
                            if matches:
                                print(f"*** POTENTIAL COMPOSER NAMES: {matches} ***")
                        
                        # Look for specific mentions of alternative composers
                        alternative_patterns = [
                            r'secondary composer',
                            r'additional music',
                            r'music team',
                            r'orchestrator',
                            r'music director',
                            r'ceremony music'
                        ]
                        
                        for pattern in alternative_patterns:
                            if re.search(pattern, combined_text, re.IGNORECASE):
                                print(f"*** ALTERNATIVE COMPOSER ROLE: {pattern} ***")
                        
                        print("-" * 60)
                
                print(f"\nCompleted search {i}/{len(search_queries)}\n")
                
            else:
                print(f"Search failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}")
                
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error during search {i}: {str(e)}")
        
        print("=" * 70)
        print()
    
    # Save all search results for detailed analysis
    comprehensive_results = {
        'search_objective': 'Find French-born composers with Pioneer Pictures connections for 1976 Montreal Olympics',
        'search_timestamp': '2024-12-19',
        'total_queries_executed': len(search_queries),
        'queries_used': search_queries,
        'all_search_results': all_search_results,
        'total_organic_results': sum([sr['organic_count'] for sr in all_search_results]),
        'search_focus': 'Alternative to AndrÃ© Mathieu (Canadian, not French)'
    }
    
    with open('workspace/alternative_composer_search_results.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        json.dump(comprehensive_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
    
    print(f"\n=== SEARCH PHASE COMPLETE ===\n")
    print(f"Total searches conducted: {len(search_queries)}")
    print(f"Total organic results collected: {comprehensive_results['total_organic_results']}")
    print(f"Results saved to: workspace/alternative_composer_search_results.json")
    
    print("\nNext steps:")
    print("1. Analyze collected results for French-born composers")
    print("2. Focus on Pioneer Pictures connections")
    print("3. Cross-reference 1976 Montreal Olympics music team")
    print("4. Identify alternative composers beyond AndrÃ© Mathieu")
    
    # Additional targeted searches for specific composer roles
    print("\n=== ADDITIONAL TARGETED SEARCHES ===\n")
    
    additional_queries = [
        "1976 Montreal Olympics music director French composer",
        "Montreal 1976 Olympics orchestrator French musician film",
        "Pioneer Pictures French composer 1970s Olympic music"
    ]
    
    for i, query in enumerate(additional_queries, 1):
        print(f"Additional Search {i}: {query}")
        
        params = {
            "q": query,
            "api_key": api_key,
            "engine": "google",
            "google_domain": "google.com",
            "safe": "off",
            "num": 10,
            "type": "search",
        }
        
        try:
            response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30)
            
            if response.status_code == 200:
                results = response.json()
                print(f"Found {len(results.get('organic_results', []))} additional results")
                
                # Quick analysis for French composers
                if results.get("organic_results"):
                    for result in results['organic_results'][:5]:
                        title = result.get('title', '')
                        snippet = result.get('snippet', '')
                        combined = f"{title} {snippet}".lower()
                        
                        if 'french' in combined and ('composer' in combined or 'music' in combined):
                            print(f"*** POTENTIAL FRENCH COMPOSER FOUND ***")
                            print(f"Title: {title}")
                            print(f"Snippet: {snippet[:150]}...")
                            print()
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error in additional search {i}: {str(e)}")
    
    print("\n=== SEARCH COMPLETE ===\n")
    print("Ready for detailed analysis of alternative French composers with Pioneer Pictures connections.")

Access the main page to understand the site structure\n    response = requests.get(base_url, headers=headers, timeout=15)\n    print(f"Main page status: {response.status_code}")\n    \n    if response.status_code == 200:\n        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n        print(f"Successfully accessed CyclingRanking.com")\n        \n        # Look for navigation links or search functionality\n        nav_links = soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True)\n        relevant_links = []\n        \n        for link in nav_links[:20]:  # Check first 20 links\n            href = link.get(\'href\', \'\')\n            text = link.get_text(strip=True)\n            \n            # Look for links related to riders, search, or historical data\n            if any(keyword in href.lower() for keyword in [\'rider\', \'cyclist\', \'search\', \'ranking\', \'history\']):\n                relevant_links.append({\'text\': text, \'href\': href})\n                print(f"Found relevant link: {text} -> {href}")\n        \n        # Look for search forms or input fields\n        search_forms = soup.find_all(\'form\')\n        search_inputs = soup.find_all(\'input\', {\'type\': [\'search\', \'text\']})\n        \n        print(f"\\nFound {len(search_forms)} forms and {len(search_inputs)} search inputs")\n        \n        for i, form in enumerate(search_forms):\n            print(f"Form {i+1}: {form.get(\'action\', \'No action\')} - Method: {form.get(\'method\', \'No method\')}")\n        \n        for i, inp in enumerate(search_inputs):\n            print(f"Input {i+1}: Name=\'{inp.get(\'name\', \'No name\')}\' Placeholder=\'{inp.get(\'placeholder\', \'No placeholder\')}\'")\n    \n    else:\n        print(f"Failed to access main page: {response.status_code}")\n        print(f"Response text: {response.text[:200]}...")\n\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"Error accessing CyclingRanking.com: {str(e)}")\n\nprint("\\nðŸ” STEP 2: Searching for French cyclists from 1928-1931 era")\nprint("-" * 50)\n\n# Known prominent French cyclists from that era to check\nfrench_cyclists_1928_1931 = [\n    "AndrÃ© Leducq",\n    "Antonin Magne", \n    "Georges Speicher",\n    "Charles PÃ©lissier",\n    "Henri PÃ©lissier",\n    "Francis PÃ©lissier",\n    "Maurice Archambaud",\n    "RenÃ© Vietto",\n    "Lucien Buysse",\n    "Gaston Rebry",\n    "Marcel Bidot",\n    "Georges Ronsse",\n    "Jef Demuysere",\n    "Learco Guerra"\n]\n\nprint(f"Target cyclists to search: {len(french_cyclists_1928_1931)}")\nfor i, cyclist in enumerate(french_cyclists_1928_1931, 1):\n    print(f"{i:2d}. {cyclist}")\n\n# Try different URL patterns to access rider profiles\nurl_patterns = [\n    "/rider/{}",\n    "/riders/{}",\n    "/cyclist/{}",\n    "/profile/{}",\n    "/search?q={}",\n    "/search?name={}"\n]\n\nprint("\\nðŸ” STEP 3: Attempting to access individual rider profiles")\nprint("-" * 55)\n\nrider_search_results = []\nsearch_attempts = 0\nsuccessful_accesses = 0\n\nfor cyclist_name in french_cyclists_1928_1931[:5]:  # Start with first 5 cyclists\n    print(f"\\nðŸš´ Searching for: {cyclist_name}")\n    print("-" * 30)\n    \n    # Create URL-friendly version of name\n    url_name = cyclist_name.lower().replace(" ", "-").replace("Ã©", "e").replace("Ã¨", "e")\n    url_name_underscore = cyclist_name.lower().replace(" ", "_").replace("Ã©", "e").replace("Ã¨", "e")\n    url_name_space = cyclist_name.replace(" ", "%20")\n    \n    name_variations = [url_name, url_name_underscore, url_name_space, cyclist_name]\n    \n    found_profile = False\n    \n    for pattern in url_patterns:\n        for name_var in name_variations:\n            if found_profile:\n                break\n                \n            try:\n                test_url = base_url + pattern.format(name_var)\n                print(f"Trying: {test_url}")\n                \n                response = requests.get(test_url, headers=headers, timeout=10)\n                search_attempts += 1\n                \n                if response.status_code == 200:\n                    soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n                    page_text = soup.get_text().lower()\n                    \n                    # Check if this looks like a rider profile page\n                    profile_indicators = [\'born\', \'nationality\', \'career\', \'victories\', \'ranking\', \'score\']\n                    indicator_count = sum(1 for indicator in profile_indicators if indicator in page_text)\n                    \n                    if indicator_count >= 2:  # Likely a profile page\n                        print(f"âœ… Found profile page for {cyclist_name}!")\n                        successful_accesses += 1\n                        found_profile = True\n                        \n                        # Look for score information\n                        score_patterns = [\n                            r\'score[:\\s]*([0-9,]+)\',\n                            r\'ranking[:\\s]*([0-9,]+)\',\n                            r\'points[:\\s]*([0-9,]+)\',\n                            r\'([0-9,]+)[\\s]*points\',\n                            r\'total[:\\s]*([0-9,]+)\'\n                        ]\n                        \n                        scores_found = []\n                        for pattern in score_patterns:\n                            matches = re.findall(pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE)\n                            for match in matches:\n                                # Clean up the score (remove commas, etc.)\n                                clean_score = re.sub(r\'[^0-9]\', \'\', match)\n                                if clean_score and len(clean_score) <= 6:  # Reasonable score length\n                                    scores_found.append(clean_score)\n                        \n                        # Check for the target score 3857\n                        if \'3857\' in scores_found:\n                            print(f"ðŸŽ¯ TARGET SCORE 3857 FOUND for {cyclist_name}!")\n                            print(f"URL: {test_url}")\n                        \n                        print(f"Scores found: {list(set(scores_found))}")\n                        \n                        # Look for career years\n                        year_patterns = [\n                            r\'(19[0-9]{2})\',\n                            r\'career[:\\s]*([0-9]{4})[\\s]*[-â€“][\\s]*([0-9]{4})\',\n                            r\'active[:\\s]*([0-9]{4})[\\s]*[-â€“][\\s]*([0-9]{4})\'\n                        ]\n                        \n                        years_found = []\n                        for pattern in year_patterns:\n                            matches = re.findall(pattern, page_text)\n                            years_found.extend([match if isinstance(match, str) else match[0] for match in matches])\n                        \n                        # Check if active in 1928-1931 period\n                        target_years = [\'1928\', \'1929\', \'1930\', \'1931\']\n                        active_in_period = any(year in years_found for year in target_years)\n                        \n                        if active_in_period:\n                            print(f"âœ… {cyclist_name} was active in 1928-1931 period")\n                        \n                        print(f"Years found: {list(set(years_found))}")\n                        \n                        # Store the result\n                        rider_result = {\n                            \'name\': cyclist_name,\n                            \'url\': test_url,\n                            \'scores_found\': list(set(scores_found)),\n                            \'years_found\': list(set(years_found)),\n                            \'has_target_score\': \'3857\' in scores_found,\n                            \'active_in_period\': active_in_period,\n                            \'page_content_sample\': page_text[:500]\n                        }\n                        \n                        rider_search_results.append(rider_result)\n                        \n                        # If we found the target score, save detailed information\n                        if \'3857\' in scores_found:\n                            detailed_file = f\'workspace/target_cyclist_found_{cyclist_name.replace(" ", "_")}.html\'\n                            with open(detailed_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                                f.write(response.text)\n                            print(f"ðŸ’¾ Saved detailed profile to: {detailed_file}")\n                        \n                        break\n                    \n                    elif response.status_code == 404:\n                        print(f"âŒ 404 Not Found: {test_url}")\n                    else:\n                        print(f"âŒ Status {response.status_code}: {test_url}")\n                        \n                time.sleep(1)  # Be respectful to the server\n                \n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f"âŒ Error accessing {test_url}: {str(e)}")\n                continue\n    \n    if not found_profile:\n        print(f"âŒ No profile found for {cyclist_name}")\n    \n    print(f"Completed search for {cyclist_name}")\n    time.sleep(2)  # Pause between cyclists\n\nprint(f"\\nðŸ“Š SEARCH SUMMARY:")\nprint(f"Total search attempts: {search_attempts}")\nprint(f"Successful profile accesses: {successful_accesses}")\nprint(f"Riders with data found: {len(rider_search_results)}")\n\n# Check if we found the target\ntarget_found = [r for r in rider_search_results if r[\'has_target_score\']]\nif target_found:\n    print(f"\\nðŸŽ¯ TARGET CYCLIST FOUND!")\n    for target in target_found:\n        print(f"Name: {target[\'name\']}")\n        print(f"URL: {target[\'url\']}")\n        print(f"Score 3857: âœ…")\n        print(f"Active 1928-1931: {\'âœ…\' if target[\'active_in_period\'] else \'âŒ\'}")\nelse:\n    print(f"\\nâŒ Target score 3857 not found in initial search")\n    print(f"Need to expand search to more cyclists or try different approaches")\n\n# Save search results\ntimestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")\nresults_file = f\'workspace/cycling_ranking_search_{timestamp}.json\'\n\nsearch_data = {\n    \'search_timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n    \'objective\': \'Find French cyclist with score 3857 active 1928-1931\',\n    \'target_website\': \'CyclingRanking.com\',\n    \'cyclists_searched\': french_cyclists_1928_1931[:5],\n    \'total_attempts\': search_attempts,\n    \'successful_accesses\': successful_accesses,\n    \'results\': rider_search_results,\n    \'target_found\': len(target_found) > 0,\n    \'target_details\': target_found if target_found else None\n}\n\nwith open(results_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(search_data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n\nprint(f"\\nðŸ’¾ Search results saved to: {results_file}")\nprint(f"\\nâœ… Initial CyclingRanking.com search phase completed!")\nprint(f"Ready to expand search if target not found or analyze successful results.")',

Target French cyclists from the specified era\n    french_cyclists_1928_1931 = [\n        "AndrÃ© Leducq",\n        "Antonin Magne", \n        "Georges Speicher",\n        "Charles PÃ©lissier",\n        "Henri PÃ©lissier",\n        "Francis PÃ©lissier",\n        "Maurice Archambaud",\n        "RenÃ© Vietto",\n        "Marcel Bidot",\n        "Gaston Rebry"\n    ]\n    \n    print(f"Target cyclists for score 3857 search: {len(french_cyclists_1928_1931)}")\n    for i, cyclist in enumerate(french_cyclists_1928_1931, 1):\n        print(f"{i:2d}. {cyclist}")\n    \n    print("\\nðŸ” STEP 3: Testing URL patterns for cyclist profiles")\n    print("-" * 50)\n    \n    # URL patterns to test for accessing cyclist profiles\n    url_patterns = [\n        "/rider/{}",\n        "/riders/{}",\n        "/cyclist/{}",\n        "/profile/{}",\n        "/search?q={}",\n        "/search?name={}",\n        "/en/rider/{}"\n    ]\n    \n    # Search results storage\n    search_results = []\n    total_attempts = 0\n    successful_profiles = 0\n    target_found = False\n    \n    # Search through first 6 cyclists systematically\n    for cyclist_name in french_cyclists_1928_1931[:6]:\n        print(f"\\nðŸš´ Searching for: {cyclist_name}")\n        print("-" * 40)\n        \n        # Create URL-friendly name variations\n        name_clean = cyclist_name.lower().replace(" ", "-").replace("Ã©", "e").replace("Ã¨", "e").replace("Ã ", "a")\n        name_underscore = cyclist_name.lower().replace(" ", "_").replace("Ã©", "e").replace("Ã¨", "e").replace("Ã ", "a")\n        name_encoded = cyclist_name.replace(" ", "%20")\n        \n        name_variations = [name_clean, name_underscore, name_encoded]\n        \n        cyclist_profile_found = False\n        \n        # Try each URL pattern with each name variation\n        for pattern in url_patterns:\n            if cyclist_profile_found:\n                break\n                \n            for name_variant in name_variations:\n                if cyclist_profile_found:\n                    break\n                    \n                try:\n                    test_url = base_url + pattern.format(name_variant)\n                    print(f"Trying: {test_url}")\n                    \n                    response = requests.get(test_url, headers=headers, timeout=10)\n                    total_attempts += 1\n                    \n                    if response.status_code == 200:\n                        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n                        page_text = soup.get_text().lower()\n                        \n                        # Check if this is a cyclist profile page\n                        profile_keywords = [\'born\', \'nationality\', \'career\', \'victories\', \'ranking\', \'score\', \'points\', \'cyclist\', \'rider\']\n                        keyword_matches = sum(1 for keyword in profile_keywords if keyword in page_text)\n                        \n                        print(f"Profile indicators: {keyword_matches}")\n                        \n                        if keyword_matches >= 3:  # Likely a profile page\n                            print(f"âœ… Found profile for {cyclist_name}!")\n                            successful_profiles += 1\n                            cyclist_profile_found = True\n                            \n                            # Search for numerical scores in the page\n                            score_patterns = [\n                                r\'score[:\\s]*([0-9,]+)\',\n                                r\'points[:\\s]*([0-9,]+)\',\n                                r\'ranking[:\\s]*([0-9,]+)\',\n                                r\'total[:\\s]*([0-9,]+)\',\n                                r\'([0-9]{4})(?![0-9])\',  # 4-digit numbers\n                                r\'3857\'  # Direct target score search\n                            ]\n                            \n                            found_scores = []\n                            for score_pattern in score_patterns:\n                                matches = re.findall(score_pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE)\n                                for match in matches:\n                                    # Clean the score (remove commas, etc.)\n                                    clean_score = re.sub(r\'[^0-9]\', \'\', str(match))\n                                    if clean_score and len(clean_score) <= 6:  # Reasonable score length\n                                        found_scores.append(clean_score)\n                            \n                            # Remove duplicates and sort\n                            unique_scores = sorted(list(set(found_scores)))\n                            \n                            # Check for the target score 3857\n                            if \'3857\' in unique_scores:\n                                print(f"ðŸŽ¯ TARGET SCORE 3857 FOUND for {cyclist_name}!")\n                                print(f"Profile URL: {test_url}")\n                                target_found = True\n                                \n                                # Show first 20 scores\n                            \n                            # Look for career years\n                            year_matches = re.findall(r\'(19[0-9]{2})\', page_text)\n                            unique_years = sorted(list(set(year_matches)))\n                            \n                            # Check if active in 1928-1931 period\n                            target_period = [\'1928\', \'1929\', \'1930\', \'1931\']\n                            active_in_target_period = any(year in unique_years for year in target_period)\n                            \n                            if active_in_target_period:\n                                print(f"âœ… Active in 1928-1931 period")\n                            else:\n                                print(f"âŒ Not active in 1928-1931 period")\n                            \n                            print(f"Career years found: {unique_years[:15]}...")  # Show first 15 years\n                            \n                            # Store the search result\n                            cyclist_result = {\n                                \'name\': cyclist_name,\n                                \'profile_url\': test_url,\n                                \'scores_found\': unique_scores[:25],  # Limit to first 25 scores\n                                \'career_years\': unique_years,\n                                \'has_target_score_3857\': \'3857\' in unique_scores,\n                                \'active_in_1928_1931\': active_in_target_period,\n                                \'profile_indicators\': keyword_matches\n                            }\n                            search_results.append(cyclist_result)\n                            \n                            break\n                        else:\n                            print(f"âŒ Not a profile page (indicators: {keyword_matches})")\n                    else:\n                        print(f"âŒ HTTP {response.status_code}")\n                    \n                    time.sleep(1)  # Respectful delay\n                    \n                except Exception as e:\n                    print(f"âŒ Error accessing {test_url}: {str(e)}")\n                    continue\n        \n        if not cyclist_profile_found:\n            print(f"âŒ No profile found for {cyclist_name}")\n        \n        print(f"Completed search for {cyclist_name}")\n        time.sleep(2)  # Pause between cyclists\n    \n    print(f"\\nðŸ“Š COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH SUMMARY")\n    print("=" * 40)\n    print(f"Total URL attempts: {total_attempts}")\n    print(f"Successful profile accesses: {successful_profiles}")\n    print(f"Cyclist results collected: {len(search_results)}")\n    \n    # Check if we found the target cyclist\n    target_cyclists = [result for result in search_results if result[\'has_target_score_3857\']]\n    \n    if target_cyclists:\n        print(f"\\nðŸŽ¯ SUCCESS: Found {len(target_cyclists)} cyclist(s) with score 3857!")\n        for target in target_cyclists:\n            print(f"\\nTarget Cyclist Details:")\n            print(f"Name: {target[\'name\']}")\n            print(f"Profile URL: {target[\'profile_url\']}")\n            print(f"Score 3857: âœ…")\n            print(f"Active 1928-1931: {\'âœ…\' if target[\'active_in_1928_1931\'] else \'âŒ\'}")\n            print(f"Career years: {target[\'career_years\'][:10]}...")  # Look for rider profile links using regex\n    link_pattern = r\'<a[^>]+href="(/rider/[^"]+)"[^>]*>([^<]+)</a>\'\n    matches = re.findall(link_pattern, html_content, re.IGNORECASE)\n    \n    for link_url, link_text in matches:\n        # Check if any part of the target name matches\n        name_match = any(name_part.lower() in link_text.lower() \n                       for name_part in target_name_parts)\n        \n        if name_match:\n            full_profile_url = website_base_url + link_url if link_url.startswith(\'/\') else link_url\n            profile_links_found.append({\n                \'text\': link_text.strip(),\n                \'url\': link_url,\n                \'full_url\': full_profile_url\n            })\n    \n    return profile_links_found\n\ndef extract_scores_simple(html_content):\n    """Extract numerical scores using simple regex"""\n    content_lower = html_content.lower()\n    \n    # Look for various score patterns in the HTML\n    score_patterns = [\n        r\'score[:\\s]*([0-9,]+)\',\n        r\'points[:\\s]*([0-9,]+)\',\n        r\'ranking[:\\s]*([0-9,]+)\',\n        r\'total[:\\s]*([0-9,]+)\',\n        r\'>([0-9]{4})<\',  # 4-digit numbers between HTML tags\n        r\'\\b([0-9]{4})\\b\',  # 4-digit numbers as word boundaries\n        r\'3857\'  # Direct target score search\n    ]\n    \n    found_scores = []\n    for pattern in score_patterns:\n        matches = re.findall(pattern, content_lower)\n        for match in matches:\n            # Clean the score (remove commas, etc.)\n            clean_score = re.sub(r\'[^0-9]\', \'\', str(match))\n            if clean_score and len(clean_score) >= 3 and len(clean_score) <= 6:\n                found_scores.append(clean_score)\n    \n    # Remove duplicates and sort\n    unique_scores = sorted(list(set(found_scores)))\n    return unique_scores\n\ndef extract_career_years_simple(html_content):\n    """Extract career years using simple regex"""\n    year_matches = re.findall(r\'\\b(19[0-9]{2})\\b\', html_content)\n    unique_years = sorted(list(set(year_matches)))\n    return unique_years\n\n# Expanded search through additional cyclists\nexpanded_results = []\ntotal_expanded_searches = 0\nsuccessful_expanded_searches = 0\nexpanded_profiles_found = 0\ntarget_found_expanded = False\ntarget_cyclist_data_expanded = None\n\nfor i, cyclist_name in enumerate(additional_cyclists, 1):\n    print(f"\\nðŸš´ [EXPANDED {i}/{len(additional_cyclists)}] Searching: {cyclist_name}")\n    print("-" * 60)\n    \n    # Display found profiles\n                for j, profile_info in enumerate(profile_links, 1):\n                    print(f"  {j}. \'{profile_info[\'text\']}\' -> {profile_info[\'url\']}")\n                \n                # Extract career years\n                                career_years = extract_career_years_simple(profile_html)\n                                target_period = [\'1928\', \'1929\', \'1930\', \'1931\']\n                                active_in_target_period = any(year in career_years for year in target_period)\n                                \n                                print(f"Career years: {career_years[:15]}...")\n                                print(f"Active 1928-1931: {\'âœ…\' if active_in_target_period else \'âŒ\'}")\n                                \n                                target_cyclist_data_expanded = {\n                                    \'name\': cyclist_name,\n                                    \'profile_url\': profile_url,\n                                    \'target_score_found\': True,\n                                    \'all_scores\': found_scores[:30],\n                                    \'career_years\': career_years,\n                                    \'active_in_1928_1931\': active_in_target_period,\n                                    \'search_variant_used\': variant\n                                }\n                            else:\n                                print(f"âŒ Target score 3857 not found in {cyclist_name}\'s profile")\n                                if found_scores:\n                                    print(f"Found scores: {\', \'.join(found_scores[:20])}...")\n                            \n                            #
